 prabhaa khetaan kaa janm 1 november, 1942 ko hua
 He earned an MA degree in philosophy from Kolkata University and a phd on 'the Existentialism of Jean Paul Sartre'
 mahaj 12 varsh kii umr se hi vah sahitya sadhana main lag gayi
 His first poem was printed in 'good Morning'

 The Reserve Bank has asked banks that inter-banking portability should be allowed in accounts where full details are available under Know Your Customer (KYC)
 is suvidha ke tahat graahakon ko apana bank khaataa bank kii kisi bhi shakha main usee bank khaataa number ke saath sthanantarit karne kii suvidha milegi

 It states that the customer should be allowed to transfer his account from one branch of the bank to another branch without any hindrance
 isamen kaha gaya he ki kevaisi jaruraton ke tahat sahi pataa paane ke liye is tarah sthanantarit hone vaale khate ke liye ghar ke pate kaa nayaa saboot hasil kiya ja saktaa he

 Under this facility, customers will get the facility to transfer their bank account to any branch of the bank with the same bank account number
 tippaniyan The Reserve Bank has said in a notification, 'banks are hereby advised that on completion of KYC details in any bank branch as long as its KYC validity remains valid for transfer of that account to any branch of the bank to be supposed

 There is hardly anyone in the world who does not like watching movies and listening to songs, but do you know when and where the first cinema was built? So we tell you about the world's first cinema
 
 
 1
 On April 14, 1894, Holland Brothers opened the first commercial motion picture house in New York City
 2
 At that time, movies were seen on a kinetoscope, and only one person could enjoy it at a time
 3
 This machine used 10 such machines in 5 parallel queues, and used to run different films in each
 4
 These 10 films were part of a movie program and were shot at Thomas Edison's film studio Black Maria
 5
 The first American copyright for a motion picture was given to Edison for Fred Ott's Sneeze
 6
 During that time the viewer could watch all the movies in a row for just 25 cents

 jai hind
 a term coined as a military greeting by Majal Abid Hasan Jafrani
 aabid aaazaad hind fouj main the

 unka tark he ki prachlit abhivadan hindu dharm or murti puja se jude hai
 He believes in Islam, which does not believe in idol worship
 saath main vah maulavee bhi hai, yani islamic shikshaayen dete hai
 In such a way how can he do this greeting
 magar ali ke batalian kii ravaayat na maanane par unhen adhikariyon ne ek notice bhej diya
 It said that overcome your small thinking
 aapasi abhivadan main 'ram ram' yaa 'jai mata di' kahie
 Because this is the rule of this battalion
